@main_light_radius = 160

# Warcraft
@main_light_height = 300

@main_light_angle = 20
@main_cubemap_intensity = 0.4
#########################################################################
#########################################################################
#																		#
#							MAIN ENVIRONMENTS							#
#																		#
#########################################################################
#########################################################################

environment_standard = {
	cubemap = "gfx/portraits/environments/castle_interior_01_fire.dds"
	cubemap_intensity = @main_cubemap_intensity

	lights = {
		#########################################################################
		#								KEY LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		0 = {
			type = "spot_light"	# Valid types are "spot_light", "point_light", and "directional_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.1 0.45 1.5 }	# Hue, saturation, value. Increase value for more intense lights
			position = cylindrical{ @main_light_radius 	@main_light_height 	30 }	# Radius, height, angle

			# For spot lights and directional lights
			look_at = { 0 0 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			# For spot lights and point lights
			radius = 1000
			falloff = 10

			# For point lights
			outer_cone_angle = 25
			inner_cone_angle = 5
		}

		#########################################################################
		#							RIGHT RIM LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		1 = {
			type = "spot_light"
			affected_by_shadow = no
			color = hsv{ 0.05 0.8 0.3 }
			position = cylindrical{ @main_light_radius 200 -120 }

			look_at = { 0 -35 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			radius = 1000
			falloff = 50

			outer_cone_angle = 18
			inner_cone_angle = 0
		}

		#########################################################################
		#							LEFT RIM LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		2 = {
			type = "directional_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.6 0.3 1.6 }
			position = cylindrical{ 200 100 -160 }

			look_at = { 0 18 0 }
		}
	}

	shadow_camera = {
		position = cylindrical { @main_light_radius 	300	30 }	# Radius, height, angle
		look_at = { 0 0	0 }
		look_at_node = {
			default = camera_torso_look_at
		}
		fov = 50
		camera_near_far = { 100 500 }
	}
}

environment_head = {

	cubemap = "gfx/portraits/environments/castle_interior_01_fire.dds"
	cubemap_intensity = @main_cubemap_intensity

	lights = environment_standard
	shadow_camera = environment_standard
}

environment_cw_west_spouse = {

	cubemap = "gfx/portraits/environments/castle_interior_01.dds"
	cubemap_intensity = 0.5

	lights = {
		#########################################################################
		#								KEY LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		0 = {
			type = "spot_light"	# Valid types are "spot_light", "point_light", and "directional_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.1 0.3 1.0 }	# Hue, saturation, value. Increase value for more intense lights
			position = cylindrical{ @main_light_radius @main_light_height 0 }	# Radius, height, angle

			# For spot lights and directional lights
			look_at = { 0 0 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			# For spot lights and point lights
			radius = 1000
			falloff = 10

			# For point lights
			outer_cone_angle = 30
			inner_cone_angle = 0
		}

		#########################################################################
		#							RIGHT RIM LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		1 = {
			type = "spot_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.6 0.3 0.4 }
			position = cylindrical{ 200 200 140 }

			look_at = { 0 -35 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			radius = 1000
			falloff = 50

			outer_cone_angle = 48
			inner_cone_angle = 0
		}

		#########################################################################
		#							LEFT RIM LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		2 = {
			type = "directional_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.6 0.3 0.4 }
			position = cylindrical{ 200 100 -140 }

			look_at = { 0 18 0 }
		}
	}

	shadow_camera = {
		position = cylindrical{ 200 100 160 }
		look_at = { 0 0 0 }
		look_at_node = {
			default = camera_torso_look_at
		}
		fov = 50
		camera_near_far = { 10 350 }
	}
}

	cubemap = "gfx/portraits/environments/frontend_mediterranean_01.dds"
	cubemap_intensity = 0.6

	lights = {
		#########################################################################
		#								KEY LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		0 = {
			type = "spot_light"	# Valid types are "spot_light", "point_light", and "directional_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.08 0.6 1.5 }	# Hue, saturation, value. Increase value for more intense lights
			position = cylindrical{ @main_light_radius 150 60 } # Radius, height, angle

			# For spot lights and directional lights
			look_at = { 0 0 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			# For spot lights and point lights
			radius = 1000
			falloff = 10

			# For point lights
			outer_cone_angle = 25
			inner_cone_angle = 0
		}

		#########################################################################

		#########################################################################

			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.1 0.5 1.0 }
			position = cylindrical	{ 160.0 200 140 }

			color = hsv{ 0.1 0.6 1.5 }
			position = cylindrical{ @main_light_radius 200 -130 }

			look_at = { 0 -37 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			radius = 1000
			falloff = 50

			outer_cone_angle = 38
			inner_cone_angle = 0
		}

		#########################################################################
		#							LEFT RIM LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		2 = {
			type = "directional_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.08 0.4 0.8 }
			position = cylindrical{ 88 50 -140 }

			look_at = { 0 18 0 }
		}
	}

	shadow_camera = {
		position = cylindrical { 150 380 30 }
		look_at = { 0 0 0 }
		look_at_node = {
			default = camera_torso_look_at
		}

		#########################################################################

			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.1 0.45 1.5 }	# Hue, saturation, value. Increase value for more intense lights
			position = cylindrical{ @main_light_radius 	@main_light_height 	30 }	# Radius, height, angle

			# For spot lights and directional lights
			look_at = { 0 0 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			# For spot lights and point lights
			radius = 1000
			falloff = 10

			# For point lights
			outer_cone_angle = 25
			inner_cone_angle = 5
		}
	}

	shadow_camera = environment_standard
}

		#########################################################################

			type = "spot_light"	# Valid types are "spot_light", "point_light", and "directional_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.1 0.45 1.5 }	# Hue, saturation, value. Increase value for more intense lights
			position = cylindrical{		100 	200 	0 }	# Radius, height, angle

			# For spot lights and directional lights
			look_at = { 0 0 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			# For spot lights and point lights
			radius = 1000
			falloff = 10

			# For point lights
			outer_cone_angle = 70
			inner_cone_angle = 5
		}

		#########################################################################
		#							RIGHT RIM LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		1 = {
			type = "spot_light"
			affected_by_shadow = no
			color = hsv{ 0.05 0.8 0.3 }
			position = cylindrical{ @main_light_radius 200 -120 }

			look_at = { 0 -35 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			radius = 1000
			falloff = 50

			outer_cone_angle = 18
			inner_cone_angle = 0
		}

		#########################################################################
		#							LEFT RIM LIGHT								#
		#########################################################################
		2 = {
			type = "directional_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.6 0.3 0.5 }
			position = cylindrical{ 88 50 200 }

			look_at = { 0 18 0 }
		}
	}

	shadow_camera = {
		position = cylindrical {	100 	200 	0 }	# Radius, height, angle
		look_at = { 0 0	0 }
		look_at_node = {
			default = camera_torso_look_at
		}
		fov = 50
		camera_near_far = { 100 500 }
	}

}

	lights = {
		#########################################################################

		#########################################################################
		0 = {
			type = "spot_light"
			affected_by_shadow = yes

			color = hsv{ 0.07 0.7 2.4 }
			position = cylindrical	{ 38 300  0 } # Radius, height, angle

			look_at = {	0 0 0 }
			# For spot lights and directional lights
			look_at = { 0 0 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = camera_torso_look_at
			}

			# For spot lights and point lights
			radius = 1000
			falloff = 10

			# For point lights
			outer_cone_angle = 15
			inner_cone_angle = 0


		}

		#########################################################################

			type = "spot_light"
			affected_by_shadow = no

			color = hsv{ 0.08 0.4 .15 }
			position = cylindrical{ 220 50 15 }

			look_at = { 0 18 0 }

			# For spot lights and directional lights
			look_at = { 0 0 0 }
			look_at_node = {
				default = bn_h_head
			}
			position_node = {
				default = bn_h_head
			}

			# For spot lights and point lights
			radius = 1000
			falloff = 10

			# For spot lights
			outer_cone_angle = 65
			inner_cone_angle = 0
		}
	}

	shadow_camera = {
		position = cylindrical { 180 100 45 }
		look_at = { 0 0 0 }
		look_at_node = {
			default = bn_h_head
		}
		position_node = {
			default = bn_h_head
		}
		fov = 50
		camera_near_far = { 100 1350 }
	}
}
